<span style="color: red;"><i>Project Entropia - Fails to retain identity since 2009</i></span><br />
<br />
<b>Harvesting was mentioned back in 2000 and the harvester tool was there</b><br />
<b>in early beta. It was powered by Future AA batteries, which were</b><br />
<b>used as "ammo" for this tool. You just aimed at plants to gather ressources.</b><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(thx to "phoenixx" and "Jane QP Doe" for additional info)</span></span>&nbsp;</b><br />
<b><br /></b>
<b>(H-50 Farmhand Alpha)</b></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi6ngIltJ2XnQy76097DkQqPPKDbrNk9k6ZlZHr-4ulYET6I2dfnl_8_2AkGrLNpaO1ItlngEkbhOeYzgBjFQyeT1y2eC_klky4-SPNradrL-Ja34gHJzJinnz4Rjhzioa8j66OJ6mn34Y/s1600/harvester.gif" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="270" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi6ngIltJ2XnQy76097DkQqPPKDbrNk9k6ZlZHr-4ulYET6I2dfnl_8_2AkGrLNpaO1ItlngEkbhOeYzgBjFQyeT1y2eC_klky4-SPNradrL-Ja34gHJzJinnz4Rjhzioa8j66OJ6mn34Y/s400/harvester.gif" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-family: &quot;papyrus&quot;;">This
 is a standard model using a close-range teleportation system to harvest
 various forms of edible plants for personal use. It was primarily 
developed as a device for basic survival in the wild as well as an 
alternative to hunting.</span></span><br />
<br />

<div>
<b>The meat extractor was there, in early beta.</b><br />
<b>It was powered by Future AA batteries, which were</b><br />
<b>used as "ammo" for this tool. You just aimed at dead mobs</b></div>
<div>
<b>to gather ressources.</b><b>&nbsp;</b><br />
<b>&nbsp;</b><b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(thx to "phoenixx" and "Jane QP Doe" for additional info)</span></span></b><br />
<br />
<br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><br /></span></span></b>
<br />
<br />
<b>(mlx-440 Meat Extractor)</b></div>
<b>&nbsp;</b><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEihZEiTp8mig9a7IeuJWYS1axlZ4JRMlannivnMYcnzatu98KQgAIHv4afu1z-BGwz1oXHhqQk_CrQv3nMSfc5AQ1gbOMuKqXL3Kv0rKYtTEtY_7B9S6VmmiS9sWrzOLjmIJUqhVXpeNnY/s1600/meatex.gif" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="318" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEihZEiTp8mig9a7IeuJWYS1axlZ4JRMlannivnMYcnzatu98KQgAIHv4afu1z-BGwz1oXHhqQk_CrQv3nMSfc5AQ1gbOMuKqXL3Kv0rKYtTEtY_7B9S6VmmiS9sWrzOLjmIJUqhVXpeNnY/s400/meatex.gif" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: yellow;">The MXL-440 is a standard field model using conventional laser technology <span style="font-family: &quot;papyrus&quot;;">to
 cut up and extract the meat before using an auto link to transfer the 
meat into the inventory. It leaves a minimum of waste, but the 
appropriate skill is required in order to operate it effectively. Like 
all Meat Extractors, the MXL-440 cannot be used as a weapon due to its 
built-in safety function.</span></span><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<b></b></div>

<b>This thing was called FC-100 Food-Mate : </b></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjyU0v5ghWzAS9h8iO6cUTECHWCqfRkE13iRYsxgrNWN3eE6rd3GCwKGQ4c2PQqTvw_8wm2o8BVV5iU2-p6zS5zFojFfs8nL7tXsGZMaYzdXVYnRo1Sez5zNDiB8gX71U3PYxKBr6fUBJY/s1600/FC-100Food-Mate.gif" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="218" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjyU0v5ghWzAS9h8iO6cUTECHWCqfRkE13iRYsxgrNWN3eE6rd3GCwKGQ4c2PQqTvw_8wm2o8BVV5iU2-p6zS5zFojFfs8nL7tXsGZMaYzdXVYnRo1Sez5zNDiB8gX71U3PYxKBr6fUBJY/s400/FC-100Food-Mate.gif" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: yellow;">This is one of the most basic field kitchen models.<span style="font-family: &quot;papyrus&quot;;">It's
 able to turn any type of raw food into cooked food, but it can't handle
 Food Packs. From this perspective it's more practical for experienced 
travelers who are used to gathering their own food in the wild as they 
go.</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">

<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhtuJP9obSd5YBw_gzchMglw2zhC11l794p5cccStBtIhKXfTKfqAuiOCiSrxmwS998qrqExCYLwQ3N_eaLb-dpWBoJextmtIjUGoESX4fkzDztbdzjhl6I1q8Q4emJgtq6PP5jz7NJG8c/s1600/PCE-50FieldMate.gif" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="324" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhtuJP9obSd5YBw_gzchMglw2zhC11l794p5cccStBtIhKXfTKfqAuiOCiSrxmwS998qrqExCYLwQ3N_eaLb-dpWBoJextmtIjUGoESX4fkzDztbdzjhl6I1q8Q4emJgtq6PP5jz7NJG8c/s400/PCE-50FieldMate.gif" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>&nbsp;</b>PCE stands for Portable Computer Enhancement and are<span style="font-family: &quot;papyrus&quot;;">the
 most common series of Com-Pad models on Calypso. They are originally 
constructed as rugged field models for extensive use in any type of 
environment and were never designed as fashionable urban items.</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiF4Gb0PyNLliEVKG4RoxhSB4eH7qUCd9nY6AvC5m0romQpBNdlyHAFv7Ql5KVrUA4ypRXouoYueS2v6247pnJ3j6Xl3mAUgAF0NWh2Xp4Nqss5yCwrsomeWZ_ttSL4bNR-AVD4ctaNqrM/s1600/pce-50+field+mate.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiF4Gb0PyNLliEVKG4RoxhSB4eH7qUCd9nY6AvC5m0romQpBNdlyHAFv7Ql5KVrUA4ypRXouoYueS2v6247pnJ3j6Xl3mAUgAF0NWh2Xp4Nqss5yCwrsomeWZ_ttSL4bNR-AVD4ctaNqrM/s1600/pce-50+field+mate.jpg" /></a></div>

<b>...but, of coouurrsseee unused to this date (08.03.2017)</b><br />

<i>Just like many, many(!) other unused textures that find their way ingame now and then.</i><br />
<i>For example as secret robot transmitter.</i><br />
<br />
<b>The Parley BEER logo got introduced with the beach hut on Treasure Island. (2006)</b><br />
<b><br />Only the logo...no beer ofc.</b><br />
<br />
<b>If you google "Parley Beer", the 1st result will be an actor named "Parley Bear" :</b><br />

<span style="font-size: xx-small;">.</span> <br />

<i>rather than a boring necessity system"</i><br />

<b>will be finally "fixed".</b><br />

does (still) not make you gain any "<i>Heavy Weapon Skills</i>". Why should it ? lol</b></div>

<div style="text-align: center;">
<b>2005, the 1st stage of taming. </b>(gone)<b></b><br />
<b></b><br />
<b><br /></b>And we got lured with phrases like :<br />
<i>"Ride your Atrox into the sunset"&nbsp; </i><br />
<br />
<br />
&nbsp;<b>From november 2005 to 2009 we could feed and brush a very small</b><br />
<b>selection of calypsos wildlife. </b><br />
<b>The Snablesnot, the Exarosaur and the Daikiba.</b><br />
<b>You could make em dance and make them do acrobatics.</b><br />
<b>Nothing else.</b><br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: small;"><b><span style="color: yellow;">(and of course skill up "Animal Taming &amp; Whip Skills" to infinity...which some of us really did)</span></b></span><br />
<br />
<b></b><br />
<i>That were 4 years and we never reached Phase 2 of taming...</i><br />
<b></b><br />
<b><br /></b>
<br />
<b>The old stables gave us the last idea of how taming could</b><br />
<b>have been...riding a Longu...</b><br />
<br />

<br />
<br />
<b>Taming got "removed" in 2009 and since then we are waiting for its return.</b><br />
<b><br /></b></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<b>Last ETA was: "Beeing re-introduced in 2012" </b>(too bad we have 2014 already)<br />
<br />
<b></b><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjGR053H4R0JKuBUFcMlofN0nj-ep015ZZYCjt5nWzxPq9SDVtcSwayxLn6RlYUCLmVQnaDDdsosRgv5AqnP9XJr1AJrr0YqIObvcKx9Q-vmc3Diw5j6SHohnq_92dT705tkoKFYXg2iUo/s1600/taming+return+2012.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="520" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjGR053H4R0JKuBUFcMlofN0nj-ep015ZZYCjt5nWzxPq9SDVtcSwayxLn6RlYUCLmVQnaDDdsosRgv5AqnP9XJr1AJrr0YqIObvcKx9Q-vmc3Diw5j6SHohnq_92dT705tkoKFYXg2iUo/s640/taming+return+2012.jpg" width="640" /></a></div>
<span style="color: yellow;"><i>In the end of 2012 Kim Timkrans said in an interview, that their goal is to re-introduce taming</i></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><i>in 2013. But to be on the safe side, he did not want to give any ETA this time...</i></span><br />
<br />
<u><span style="color: yellow;">As of May 2013, Kim said in an interview, that the fishing-system as well as</span></u><br />
<u><span style="color: yellow;">the taming system only exists on paper. No ETA!</span></u><br />
<br />
<span style="color: lime;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: lime;"><span style="font-size: large;"><u><b><u>2014-06-02</u></b> </u></span></span><br />
<span style="color: lime;"><b><span style="font-size: large;"><u>Taadaaaa, taming probably introduced once again... </u></span><span style="font-size: small;"><u> </u></span></b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">Mindark once again announced various stages of taming.</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">It might probably start at the end of 2014. Or somewhere in 2015.&nbsp;</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">Who knows.</span></span><br />

<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">Together with taming, once again the announcement</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">of a political system showed up, as well</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">as the gazzillionth re-re-redesign of the</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">so called "social interface". Yay !</span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">No CCS octagon and no battle octagons made it into the</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">game yet. Planned for late 2014 and early 2015,</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: small;">we now have 3/2017. </span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"></span><br />
What we got "out of nowhere" is a "Battle Simulator".<br />
<br />
<b>Announced at the end of january 2017.</b><br />
<b>Released at the end of february 2017.&nbsp;@_@</b> <br />
<br />
<br />
A simple "Quake" clone in prototype stage,<br />
with glitches and bugs, noone asked for...<br />
<br />
In the end its nothing different then the "gauntlet" we already have<br />
and early pr-images of it had the name "gauntlet" in it.<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhWsmvG6tbKVCMi-1T_D3fiS_qg8vOWHvzc5UkY_haq-R_9EE4CSRCaTQyMHVxKVzbwzqsZeHlmFBhhRTqjoTSt5tEtnn3EpuZvCYxV50kpxJbqRtIrisbDkBg2ytzqTsx5qBBx4a2_Amo/s1600/battlesimulator+screenshot.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="216" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhWsmvG6tbKVCMi-1T_D3fiS_qg8vOWHvzc5UkY_haq-R_9EE4CSRCaTQyMHVxKVzbwzqsZeHlmFBhhRTqjoTSt5tEtnn3EpuZvCYxV50kpxJbqRtIrisbDkBg2ytzqTsx5qBBx4a2_Amo/s400/battlesimulator+screenshot.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>&nbsp;Avoid getting hit by the white "energy balls"</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>and shoot robots and</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>stationary turrets, that can actually evade,</b></span><br />
<span style="color: red;"><span style="color: yellow;"><b>in this linear...prototype shooter.</b></span> </span><br />
<br />
You have to pay 4 PED to be able to play it. <br />
Equipped with a rocket launcher and<br />
an energyball cannon. <br />
<br />
If you die or get screwed by a glitch on the map,<br />
you get nothing.<br />
<br />
If you manage to survive,<br />
you get the chance to open a box,<br />
that contains random loot (1.60 PED to xxx PED)<br />
<br />
Each week the "fastest" 3 players on the leaderboard<br />
get payed the "jackpot". <br />

<h3>
<span style="color: lime;"><span style="color: blue;"><u><b><span style="color: white;"><span style="color: yellow;">And about the political system :</span></span></b></u></span></span></h3>
<span style="color: blue;"><b><span style="color: white;"><span style="color: yellow;">A voting process of "The president of virtual reality"&nbsp;</span></span></b></span><br />
<span style="color: blue;"><b><span style="color: white;"><span style="color: yellow;">got initiated by MindArk in january of 2016.</span></span></b></span><br />
<span style="color: blue;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: blue;"><b><span style="color: white;"><span style="color: yellow;">You had to pay 1000$ to be able to get voted.</span></span></b></span><br />
<span style="color: blue;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: blue;"><b><span style="color: white;"><span style="color: yellow;">Only Neverdie "applied", the voting process never got&nbsp;</span></span></b></span><br />
<span style="color: blue;"><b><span style="color: white;"><span style="color: yellow;">initiated as promised...and went Oblivion. </span></span></b></span><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

<b><span style="color: white;">17.06.2016</span></b><br />
<b><span style="color: white;">New elected community liaison by Mindark is Nighthawk.</span></b><br />
<b><span style="color: white;">His 1st post was :</span></b><br />
<b><span style="color: white;"><br /></span></b>
<b><span style="color: white;">The MindArk management team has reviewed the proposal made by the 
President of Virtual Reality concerning teleporter fees, and has 
determined that such a system does not complement the current 
development plans for Entropia Universe and therefore will not be 
implemented. </span>
<span style="color: white;"><br />
However, the proposal was very interesting, and aspects of it may find 
their way into future planned systems and features where participants 
would be more receptive to optional fees that provide enhanced 
convenience and utility.</span></b><br />

Compet(z) finally got released as beta on <b>May 17, 2016</b>.<br />
A mix of pet fighting, Hearthstone and "<i>Win money to cash it out"</i>.<br />
Made with the unity engine.<br />
MindArks main game, Entropia Universe itself, had to suffer badly from it<br />
over the past 2 years. As if it wasnt suffering enough by now.<br />
<br />

<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Many of us "own" Compet Deeds since 2014.&nbsp;</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Deeds that are supposed to make us earn revenue.</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>We havent gotten any revenue since 2014.&nbsp;</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Its now 3 / 2017.</b></span><br />
<br />
1st beta of "Compet" got announced for Q1 2016.<br />
1st payouts should have arrived around the end of 2016.<br />
(30%) <br />
<br />
Then 1st payouts got announced for january 2017.<br />
<br />
Then 1st payouts got announced for late february 2017.<br />
<br />
Its now march 2017.<br />
<br />
Sitting 3 years on deeds doing nothing.<br />
<br />
On the 25th february 2018, the deeds payed out.<br />
0.35 PED (35 pec) per deed...in 1 year.<br />
So it will take you 300 years to get back what you payed<br />
once for 1 deed - 100 ped (later 120 PED)<br />
<br />
In the meantime MindArk took 2 million dollars of<br />
its loyal community, paying an undisclosed sum<br />
to N-IX...to create Compet.<br />
<br />

<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Around 2006 MindArk announced the introduction of "Ageia PhysX".</b></span><br />
An additional PCI card for your PC would enable :<br />
-stuntcar vehicles with visible damage<br />
-weapons affecting the environment<br />
-Awesome "clothes in the wind" effects <br />
-Volcano with flowing lava<br />
etc.<br />

<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="color: #444444;"><span style="color: yellow;">Meanwhile Neverdie decided to sell his CND to John Foma Kalun (pesok) in<i> </i>july of 2010.</span> </span></span><br />
</b><br />
<b></b><br />
<b><i>&nbsp;</i></b><b><i>&nbsp; </i><span style="font-size: small;"><i><u><span style="font-size: small;">And then, out of nowhere<span style="font-size: small;">,</span></span> in february of 2011 :</u></i></span>&nbsp;</b><br />
<br />
<b><b>CND...ahem, F.O.M.A. Stadium has finally arrived ! Wohoooo...</b></b><br />
<b>...you can now drive your vehicle on a 2003 styled 3D track !</b><br />

<b>right after the hangars got re-introduced in april of 2011.</b><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(Hangars<span style="font-size: x-small;"> and its shuttles</span> started to bec<span style="font-size: x-small;">o</span>me useless<span style="font-size: x-small;"> around VU 10[august of 2009]</span>)</span></span> </b><br />

<b>Spacetravel is possible with cheap spaceships since june of 2011.</b><br />
<b>Spaceships, everybody can afford and everybody can travel through space with...</b><br />
<b>...no more hangars needed.</b><br />

<u><b>Massive Ads was contracted by MindArk in March of 2006.</b></u><br />
<i>(To bring tons of realworld advertisements ingame.)</i><br />
<b>2 months later, may of 2006, arch-enemy Microsoft bought Massive Ads</b>,<br />
<b>just to shut it down in 2010.</b><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b><i>(<span style="color: black;"><span style="color: yellow;">So,</span> </span>Massive Ads is no longer existing since 2010)</i></b></span><br />

<span style="color: yellow;"><b>But till August of 2012 MindArk was still hyping their</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>"reallife advertisements <i>v</i>ia massive ads"</b></span><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both;">

<u><b>MindArk partnered with Sometrics in 2012.</b></u><br />
You could do surveys and watch videos to gain pecs.<br />
Last entry of www.sometrics.com on the waybackmachine<br />
is dated Oct. 2014 and the site is down.<br />

Got bought by American Express in 2011.<br />
Partnered with MindArk in 2012.<br />
and shutdown in 2014.<br />

<b><span style="font-size: 12px;"><b><a class="externalLink" href="https://deeptoken.io/#collapse-2-sale" target="_blank">Why is there no Pre-Sale for DeepToken?</a></b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><u>MindArk wishes to allow equal opportunity for investment in DTA. We feel
 that distribution of DTA in discounted pre-sales or air-drops devalues 
the investments of those supporting MindArks vision.</u></span></b><br />

<div style="text-align: center;">
<b>Somewhere in 2009 a gigantic, well designed golf course got introduced...</b><br />
<b>...non functional of course.</b></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<b>It got removed then, because it was considered "a step into the wrong direction".</b><br />
<br />
<b>It was (and still is) called "Athena Space Port" and looks like this now (2013-2017) :</b><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi5XEo1JGKfJpDerYNvWt27N0kXvXWMc96PdWA8tU04JqZwmjpY4NIj1MwDuso89kD5mVey9v3KOrcisfiVL0cpe00wnUIvAdKedMwc-ghwVdKqJzi7P1o5kCSM7Wx-1c5UeIFbGOwHYFQ/s1600/athena+golf+new.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="360" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi5XEo1JGKfJpDerYNvWt27N0kXvXWMc96PdWA8tU04JqZwmjpY4NIj1MwDuso89kD5mVey9v3KOrcisfiVL0cpe00wnUIvAdKedMwc-ghwVdKqJzi7P1o5kCSM7Wx-1c5UeIFbGOwHYFQ/s640/athena+golf+new.jpg" width="640" /></a></div>
<b><i>It has the size of Port Atlantis and is usually empty. Noone there. Nothing to do there.</i> </b></div>

<br />
<b>Which
 reminds me of the new scanner sound and graphic effects... almost as 
scary as our critical hit "Mickey Mouse" dong sound...</b><br />
<br />
<b>There was no need at all to exchange the stylish sound of scanning,</b><br />
<b>adding a terrible kindergarten animation...to <span style="font-size: small;">where was</span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-size: small;">no animation at all before.</span></b></div>
<br />
<br />
<br />
<b><br /></b>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEghmadUPXqOiJTgYbL7oY-GWM281VsvdcBnmPI9YIFJTz9qVaD0V6WA4QvxmEbeIhUZJyrJDe6F7F7M4F4nz7L5NNyVJWt3CRD3og0onHGFfhw377JQ0TITnANl7LLa2w19L4ECMArt1z0/s1600/investafoe.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="163" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEghmadUPXqOiJTgYbL7oY-GWM281VsvdcBnmPI9YIFJTz9qVaD0V6WA4QvxmEbeIhUZJyrJDe6F7F7M4F4nz7L5NNyVJWt3CRD3og0onHGFfhw377JQ0TITnANl7LLa2w19L4ECMArt1z0/s400/investafoe.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<br />
<b>With the recent changes of "Scanning", all professions that are connected to it,</b><br />
<b>became more or less useless.&nbsp;</b><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(Did someone say those profession just went to Oblivion ?)</span></span> </b><br />
<br />
<b>From 2004 to 2010 you could scan one enemy forever.</b><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(Hell, the thing is even called "Invest-a-Foe" !)</span></span></b><br />
<b>And it felt right to gather as much informations (skills) about</b><br />
<b>one enemy as possible. After all WE pay(ed) the decay.</b><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">( In todays Entropia you can scan <span style="font-size: x-small;">an</span> enemy only once<span style="font-size: x-small;">.</span>)</span></span></b><br />
<br />
<b>There are even 4 main professions connected to scanning,</b><br />
<b>wich can make you unlock even more scanning related skills !</b><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(not anymore...you will SEE why, when you read on)</span></span><br />
<br />
<b>The<span style="font-size: x-small;"> <span style="font-size: small;">professions</span></span> are<span style="font-size: x-small;"> :</span> Humanoid/Animal/Mutant and Robot - Investigator and</b><br />
<b>after the "nerf" we even got Technology Investigator</b><br />
<br />
<b>&nbsp;<u>Problem 1 :</u> <span style="font-size: small;">&nbsp;</span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">I</span>f </span>you want to scan A LOT,&nbsp;</b><br />
<b>you would probably have to enter a mob<span style="font-size: small;">/robot</span> filled area to do that.</b><br />
<br />
<b><u>Problem 2 :</u></b><br />
<b>You are probably not going to survive the hordes of mobs<span style="font-size: small;">/robots</span>,</b><br />
<b>without wearing a hig-end armor, ending up with lots of decay<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;">, probably</span></span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;">not worth the scannin<span style="font-size: small;">g</span> skills you got. </span></span></b><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b><span style="font-size: x-small;">(Sure, you could follow an expirienced hunter all day long,</span></b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b><span style="font-size: x-small;">hoping that he will protect you and not getting angry because you</span></b></span><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">just lured in 2 <span style="font-size: x-small;">additional mobs)</span></span></span></b><br />
<br />
<b><u>Problem 3 :</u> </b><br />
<b>The way scanning "works" now, you will probably never reach&nbsp;</b><br />
<b>the needed levels to unlock the following hidden skills :</b><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b><span style="font-size: x-small;">(trust me, you wont)</span></b></span><br />
<br />
<br />
<b>Xenobiology - </b>Level 30 Animal or Mutant investigator<b></b><br />

<br />
<br />
At least the community stays together now and then and came up<br />
with a "<i>Scanning Event</i>". Hundreds of vehicles dropped in a huge circle.<br />
<br />
While walking around and scanning each vehicle, enough time passes<br />
between the 1st and last vehicle you scanned and<br />
you could scan all day long.<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(I was told it is possible unlocking robotology this way. But such events do not</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">happen every day and they wont help unlocking xenobiology either.)</span></span><br />
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;"><br /></span></i></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">I made a test with luck, using the free beacon out of Port Atlantis</span></i><br />
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">as a Scanner-Paradise:</span></i><br />
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">I nearly scanned all of the "gazzillion" robots in there</span></i><br />
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">and received 4 skills at all. </span></i><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">&nbsp;</span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(2x Scan Robot Skill,<span style="font-size: x-small;"> 1x Mechanics, 1x Analysis)</span></span></span><br />

<br />
<u><b>Which reminds me of the shop-de<span style="font-size: small;">sign</span> competition...</b></u></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br />
In 2009 Mindark...ahem...FPC...wait it was "SEE Digital Studios" then,<br />
but changed to "AR Universe AB"...then to "Planet Calypso AB"...<br />
...whatever, a competition got started :<br />
<br />
<i>"Who will design the funkiest ingame shop?"</i> <br />
<b><br /></b>
<b>1st prize would have been a full set of unlimited Martial Armor (SGA Edition)</b><br />
<b><br /></b>
<b>2nd to 5th prize would have been a full set of a unlimited Vigilante Armor (SGA Edition)</b><br />
<br />
People started decorating, bought additional (funky) items and uploaded (funky) images to<br />
their ingame ad-screens <span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(for additional fees of course)</span></span>.<br />
<br />
Every shop owner tried to design the best shop !<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">(Some even invested 30.000 PED into this competition...others "only" 2000 PED)</span></span> <br />
<br />
The problem is, no jury were ever choosing a winner,<br />
hence no prizes were ever handed out<span style="font-size: x-small;">.</span><br />
<br />
But its not the fault of Mindark...ahem...FPC...I mean "SEE Digital Studios", no,<br />
"AR Universe AB"......well, its "Planet Calypso AB" now...<br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;">Poor Hanne had to post on the forum 7 months later (2010), telling the ppl the competition will be re-vived,&nbsp;</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">and the only problem is/was that people still had&nbsp;</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">problems with some furniture... o_O</span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;">And her next comment was posted in early 2011, claiming that there</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">are still problems with pc-signs...and they were still waiting for MindArk</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">to fix it...</span><br />
<br />
<b>Btw., it is still topic on the "Planet Calypso Site" :</b><br />
<br />

<b>__________________________________________</b><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<b>MindArk announced the "Landplot System" in early 2015.</b><br />
<br />
You could turn your CLD into a CLD(x) and get a piece of land,<br />
to build "something" on it. You needed additional items as well,<br />
to be able to start building. </div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: yellow;">Start requirements for largest Plot is 162 CLDs :D (162*150$ =<b> 24.300$)</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>+additional items to start building</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>+later decoration and bazaar items</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>around 30.000 $. </b></span><br />
<i><br />
Each settlement features a large bazaar in the center as well as service
 centers on the outskirts and small 10x10m plots for monuments and other
 functions.</i><br />
<br />
<u><b>A preview looked promising :</b></u><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

<b><span style="color: yellow;">This "system" is in silent mode since 1 year now. (May 2016).&nbsp;</span></b><br />
<b><span style="color: yellow;">No further announcements or updates have been made. </span></b><br />

<b>Silence.</b><br />
After the interface got "introduced on 29.6.2016, it was silent for another 3 months.<br />
Then MA announced "gardening" on 24.9.2016 as "one of the things" for<br />
their next update.<br />

<br />
Will this system get ignored soon ?<br />
Just like many of the other things that got lsot in time by now ?<br />
We will SEE...<br />

<div style="text-align: center;">
<b>There was a NASA MMO contest in 2008, but MindArk did NOT win the competition.</b></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<b>Project Whitecard Studios though, is (still) involved into it, as they and Virtual Heroes</b><br />
<b>won the NASA contest. (2008)</b><br />
<b>They planned to release a beta in 2012 and the full product in 2013.</b><br />
<b><span style="font-size: xx-small;">(Since 2nd of april 2013 the closed beta <span style="font-size: xx-small;">i</span>s running with at least 900 participants, according to their s<span style="font-size: xx-small;">ite</span>)</span> </b><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Astronaut:_Moon,_Mars_and_Beyond</span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="color: black;">the full game is to be expected in late 2014 now.</span>&nbsp;</span></span><b><span style="color: yellow;"> </span></b><br />
<br />
<br />
<b>Maybe thats why MindArk just partnered with Project Whitecard in 2012 then ?</b><br />
<b>To still get a p</b><b>iece of the cake ?&nbsp;</b><br />

<b>that can be used to craft on your smartphone,&nbsp;</b><br />

<b>And what happened to the ESA Project then </b><i>(March 2009)</i><b> ?</b><br />

<b>But we never heard of it again. </b><br />

<b><span style="font-size: small;">Day and nightcycles existed as an option inside the old vote terminals</span></b><b><span style="font-size: small;"> in the year 2005.&nbsp;</span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-size: small;">(4 hours daylight / 4 hours night-time)</span></b><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi1cCOWUFDFq4kXVhydEgabp3NHENWEGN4twVVT8KwYf2P3J7IcfwLp9XljJtu9PC-2zBE8OackXG7mop_NP5dUcR2MfeBqCfA3CrxrCYYIBpEWBdEKiHjMjW3A2OhSPYyr6en5_Fl9ZC4/s1600/moon.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="250" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEi1cCOWUFDFq4kXVhydEgabp3NHENWEGN4twVVT8KwYf2P3J7IcfwLp9XljJtu9PC-2zBE8OackXG7mop_NP5dUcR2MfeBqCfA3CrxrCYYIBpEWBdEKiHjMjW3A2OhSPYyr6en5_Fl9ZC4/s1600/moon.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<br />
<br />
When day and nightcycles got introduced,<br />
people actually started to complain,<br />
that it is "too dark" at night... ! (wtf ?)<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;">(maybe also because MA was not able to introduce somekind of flashlights, except for vehicle lights)</span><br />
<br />
So, now we have a gigantic shiny moon and not-so-dark nights,<br />
that are even shorter.<br />
<br />
Once 5 hours of night-time, turned into 2 hours. (2012)<br />
And now we have 20 minutes of night-time. (nearly no darkness)<br />
No chance for the once announced, nocturnal mobs.<br />
<br />
Day and Nightcycles went to Oblivon, Id say...<br />
<br />

<b>Oxford/ Vexed Generations :</b> (unfinished/bankrupt)</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEj1pjv6Mb4iMo2idWcoc19eB3mCv6pjE8RTV4NzJyObNR1K6wlmigMEaciyYxkOqdTsRWTAf2eGk5vI8IkNjsigkITdd4UEw3sntl5OgmYcQCeyNZcliI66535LSFZQzRIg3sOARmPcLYQ/s1600/oxford.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="200" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEj1pjv6Mb4iMo2idWcoc19eB3mCv6pjE8RTV4NzJyObNR1K6wlmigMEaciyYxkOqdTsRWTAf2eGk5vI8IkNjsigkITdd4UEw3sntl5OgmYcQCeyNZcliI66535LSFZQzRIg3sOARmPcLYQ/s400/oxford.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: yellow;">A whole town dedicated to reallife artists like Mark Kostabi,</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">where you could buy virtual art for your virtual appartment.&nbsp;</span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;">(Introduced with VU 8.3 in 2006) </span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;">It also had a underground&nbsp; cave filled with the Boorum mob (Torkels Tomb) and</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">various shops by players. All got removed, except for the (now dead) town itself.</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: yellow;">You could also buy reallife clothes there from</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">"Vexed Generations".</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: yellow;">Vexed Generations was exisitng since 1997 and went bankrupt</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">right after it joined Entropia. Another coincidence ?</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">Vexed got removed from Entropia then.</span><br />
<br />
<br /></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">

<b>The Orbs :</b> (gone)</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgoFSnaoCl8B0PpG0h0mi0tFTvy8ONLbXk2mV1QEi5ETNJs38VFLQpWgDJtsvzFjJqB2ZMBoYPMIjAahyphenhyphentYmA2px7HFErgZLH57L__IXn8Z5RZX_9ppDDFFj6rueGpfRL-9F2LRYplv4iM/s1600/orb1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="400" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgoFSnaoCl8B0PpG0h0mi0tFTvy8ONLbXk2mV1QEi5ETNJs38VFLQpWgDJtsvzFjJqB2ZMBoYPMIjAahyphenhyphentYmA2px7HFErgZLH57L__IXn8Z5RZX_9ppDDFFj6rueGpfRL-9F2LRYplv4iM/s400/orb1.jpg" width="379" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="color: yellow;">Ya ya, it was connected to a swedish TV series</span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="color: yellow;">and MindArk got some<span style="font-size: x-small;"> prize for it...</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: small;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-size: small;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-size: small;"><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">http://www.mindark.com/press/press-releases/documents/Entropia_Universe_Is_First_Virtual_World_To_Contribute_To_Emmy_Award.pdf</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: small;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-size: small;"><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">The show was called "</span></span></span><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;"><i>The Truth About Marika". </i>We had orbs ingame</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: small;"><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: xx-small;">and viewers could log into Entropia to&nbsp; loot hints about the TV show.</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><br /></span></span></span>
<br />
<div data-canvas-width="408.22748293898593" style="font-family: sans-serif; left: 120.001px; top: 743.778px; transform: scaleX(0.923592);">
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">This partnership was a breakthrough for television </span></i></div>
<div data-canvas-width="369.8659808264264" style="font-family: sans-serif; left: 528.202px; top: 743.778px; transform: scaleX(0.904318);">
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">and the Internet in terms of creating real value </span></i></div>
<div data-canvas-width="409.40970153775714" style="font-family: sans-serif; font-size: 20px; left: 120.001px; top: 766.778px; transform: scaleX(0.934725);">
<i><span style="font-size: x-small;">for the viewers, and engaging them in multiple platforms through one program.</span></i></div>

<span style="font-size: large;"><b>Our very own solar system...went to Oblivion :</b></span><br />

<br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;">MindArk's Sayah <span style="font-size: small;">K</span>ing trailer from 2002 <span style="font-size: small;">has not lost its charme yet.</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Sometimes, over the<span style="font-size: small;"> years, <span style="font-size: small;">MindArk</span> w<span style="font-size: small;">as</span> talking about a new</span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">render trailer to be announced...one day...</span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">In the meantime, me and dub won the <span style="font-size: small;">"Create a trailer"</span> contest of 2006 :</span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">[The Video is called, "The Tru<span style="font-size: small;">th"] ^^</span> </span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="266" mozallowfullscreen="mozallowfullscreen" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/gDYpVn3vzGo?feature=player_embedded" webkitallowfullscreen="webkitallowfullscreen" width="320"></iframe></div>
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><br /></span></span></span></span>
<b><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></b><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Time passed<span style="font-size: small;"> and in 200<span style="font-size: small;">7 <span style="font-size: small;">David Simmonds called me via phone,</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">to <span style="font-size: small;">talk about a "<span style="font-size: small;">little Project they were working on"<span style="font-size: small;">.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Something like "Red vs<span style="font-size: small;">. Blue"</span> from the Halo series.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Sounded fun, but<span style="font-size: small;"> it never became reality, as I was <span style="font-size: small;">a one man army.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">I asked about a new trailer</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">and he mentioned that they were <span style="font-size: small;">indeed working on a new render trailer<span style="font-size: small;"> already.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Its 2017 now and <span style="font-size: small;">w</span>e<span style="font-size: small;"> </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>never got <span style="font-size: small;">a new render trailer<span style="font-size: small;">.</span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">In 2012 they partnered with "<span style="font-size: small;">P</span>lanet Arkadia Team<span style="font-size: small;">" though, to announce&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">that they (<span style="font-size: small;">Planet Arkadia?) </span>are finally<span style="font-size: small;"> </span>creat<span style="font-size: small;">ing</span> a new trailer for "Entropia Universe"<span style="font-size: small;">.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Again with a real actor, as Sayah <span style="font-size: small;">K</span>ing.&nbsp;</span> </span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">It was planned to <span style="font-size: small;">release the trailer a<span style="font-size: small;">round november</span> of 2012<span style="font-size: small;">.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">That ETA failed and it was planned to release it<span style="font-size: small;"> </span></span>in early 2013.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<u><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">On april 17th<span style="font-size: small;"> of 2013,</span> David Dobson informed me :</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></u><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;">Yep it's still in development, hopefully not too much longer now .</span></span></i></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: yellow;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i>It seems the new official video trailer is out now (5.7.2013).</i></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i>Using a not-so professional female voice that uses a not-so professional microphone.</i></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i>It still mentiones taming as a useable profession</i></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i>and all in all it doesnt really have the look and feel of an Official Concept Video.</i></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i>Feels more like a fan-made video,</i></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><span style="font-size: small;"><i>which isnt that bad then. ;)</i></span></span></span></span></span></span><br />

<br />
<span style="font-size: small;"><b>On April 11, 2012,</b></span><br />
<span style="font-size: small;"><b>Mindark started the "Emissary Program".</b></span><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgCGpYTdLkostlk9_gsWtJaCFy9sE7Yp-tHgBI3erxMi8dEODWVIr28MxdvqIjkJYCQwmllwwlsrFQoQGGXtunNPAO6fSpeztZSqc5jUHnqq13C3QRWkLob6PJjl3yeWX8U_XIOJjJEmR0/s1600/Entropia_Emissary_Entropia_League_of_Planets.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgCGpYTdLkostlk9_gsWtJaCFy9sE7Yp-tHgBI3erxMi8dEODWVIr28MxdvqIjkJYCQwmllwwlsrFQoQGGXtunNPAO6fSpeztZSqc5jUHnqq13C3QRWkLob6PJjl3yeWX8U_XIOJjJEmR0/s320/Entropia_Emissary_Entropia_League_of_Planets.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhYSBvrnf0hhNOXUHAyQNPe7QLh6VuA1DCniB4F_6hHGLDKoy-58wXMcQxjpxW-8SqmwW726Q1SocjSaHP-H8VaqTqim6R2kwLitblie6m3fVNsXpHpgob3Cp6wGpCTvYzovXmy1NB_1kc/s1600/emissary1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="261" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhYSBvrnf0hhNOXUHAyQNPe7QLh6VuA1DCniB4F_6hHGLDKoy-58wXMcQxjpxW-8SqmwW726Q1SocjSaHP-H8VaqTqim6R2kwLitblie6m3fVNsXpHpgob3Cp6wGpCTvYzovXmy1NB_1kc/s320/emissary1.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<br />
<br />
<b>An app on facebook, that was meant for noobs to ask</b><br />
<b>the "alpha players" for advice.&nbsp;</b><br />
<b><br /></b>
<b>You could do surveys or answer ingame questions, to level up</b><br />
<b>and win prizes...</b><br />
<br />
<b>...prizes that never got released by MindArk,&nbsp;</b><br />
<b>as this system got shut down in the same year already</b><br />
<b>and never was fully working anyway.</b><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjsohScDq34QzXzg7pE4Lqee2C51Ep68IDAukpieeHvUrytrNL_1npqT3Gz9WdpovgAMMfYsV-llVxzoUt9o66DI0fjGYfc_TfG0avVBxruFhuiWTADSBkJ-31myQSvxAj0K6aiC2yJQ-4/s1600/emissary2.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="215" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjsohScDq34QzXzg7pE4Lqee2C51Ep68IDAukpieeHvUrytrNL_1npqT3Gz9WdpovgAMMfYsV-llVxzoUt9o66DI0fjGYfc_TfG0avVBxruFhuiWTADSBkJ-31myQSvxAj0K6aiC2yJQ-4/s400/emissary2.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>

<b>The Cyber Recreation District <span style="font-size: small;">(CRD) </span>in Beijing had big plans with MindArk for sure.</b><br />
<b>Shopping planets for example. A 3D ebay, like MindArk dreamed of in 2001. </b><br />
<br />
<b>The contract got signed in oct. 2007, but then main developer, <span style="font-size: small;">Chi Tau </span>Robert Lai,&nbsp;</b><br />
<b>died on June 29, 2008,</b><br />
<b>and everything got put on hold...or canceled...who knows...</b><br />
<br />
<b>CR<span style="font-size: small;">D</span> is/<span style="font-size: small;">w</span>as also working with Master&#173;Card, Visa and the China Everbright Bank
 to build a financial platform, with suppliers like IBM.<span style="font-size: x-small;"> (hence the B<span style="font-size: x-small;">ank logo I think<span style="font-size: x-small;">)</span></span></span> </b></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">

3D Chinese shopping planets...<br />

<b>In 2009 MindArk got granted a real banking license to operate</b><br />
<b>MindBank AB as a..real bank.</b><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjaaWjI40RZpCurCmR3Vf02sX435dogomhMvSow_2MxLnVhoMgUTNyn1ybV_s-26rfCvHmC8gRShIE8PtwxA4N6J4bzz7glSbYC-GyuIJPurl_nbzomG0EbUN-XV5pSc1DTQYu_eJFY_LQ/s1600/mindbank.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="127" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjaaWjI40RZpCurCmR3Vf02sX435dogomhMvSow_2MxLnVhoMgUTNyn1ybV_s-26rfCvHmC8gRShIE8PtwxA4N6J4bzz7glSbYC-GyuIJPurl_nbzomG0EbUN-XV5pSc1DTQYu_eJFY_LQ/s400/mindbank.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<b><br /></b>
<b>It was revealed that Mind Bank failed to secure the required fundings 
for the venture (which was a sum of EUR 5 million), and thus MindArk 
requested for the permission to be revoked.</b></div>
<div>
<b><br /></b>
<span style="color: yellow;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">http://www.entropiaplanets.com/wiki/MindArk#Banking_License</span></span><b><br /></b></div>
<div>
<b><br /></b></div>
<b>Around 2015 David Simmonds (MA) claimed in an video interview</b><br />
<b>&nbsp;on a bitcoin conference, that they have still plans to "start" the bank.</b><br />
<b>Probably a prepaid-card with their logo on it...we will probably never SEE it.</b><br />
<b><span style="font-size: x-small;">(but you can SEE it up there, its called cashcard ^^)</span> </b><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;">In combination with their Deeptoken Scam, MindArk announced,</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">that if they should sell Deptokens worth 10.000.000 $ (ten million), they would</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">create the MindBank again...using the money for...research...</span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;">...even if they had the license in 2009 already...makes you wonder ?</span><br />

<b>But alas...it never went live...</b><br />
<b>...but forget about that for now,</b><br />

<b><br /></b>
<b>Neverdie brought SEE to MindArk and was heavily involved on Planet Michael development,</b><br />
<b>just like he was involved in the development of Next Island...</b><br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;">(and ofc RockTropia. And so on...) ;)</span><b></b><br />
<b><br /></b>
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>SEE Virtual Studios even bought Planet Calypso (</b><i>6 million $</i><b>) and took over its employees in january of 2011</b><b> ! </b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Then guess what...something went wrong.&nbsp;</b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>SEE only payed the 1st of 6 installments a 1 million $.</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Then, because of swedish law, MA got Calypso back and</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>sold it to its own playerbase instead.&nbsp;</b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b><span style="font-size: x-small;"><span style="color: black;">http://www.planetcalypsoforum.com/forums/showthread.php?229220-MAs-Annual-Financial-Report-for-2011 </span></span></b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b><br /></b>
<b>SEE Virtual Studios left and dismissed most, if not all of the old Calypso employees.</b></span><b> <span style="color: yellow; font-size: small;">(june 2011)</span></b><br />

<span style="color: yellow;"><b>In February 2016 MindArk announced a "2 way authentication system"</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>which would be released as app for Smartphones</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>and will natively integrate Google Authenticator.</b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>8 months later (9/2016) a "preview" version of it appears</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>on the android market and then on the Swedish IOS Store.</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b></b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b></b></span><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhz8L5y6i6oR8PqxHOIMqIcWBHAEe13i37wBRsAyimqWhKiJOh5-UBEDSgK5UYB6QLbETbLGOTVFZU15xa4D8NHRfrF_q3wZdlN3ADg3bWaiwZdn6HsuU_sMDw9O6BCVcx2lfS_Bc4zS08/s1600/2+way+auth+app+pocket.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="618" data-original-width="694" height="284" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhz8L5y6i6oR8PqxHOIMqIcWBHAEe13i37wBRsAyimqWhKiJOh5-UBEDSgK5UYB6QLbETbLGOTVFZU15xa4D8NHRfrF_q3wZdlN3ADg3bWaiwZdn6HsuU_sMDw9O6BCVcx2lfS_Bc4zS08/s320/2+way+auth+app+pocket.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<span style="color: yellow;"><b></b></span><br />
<br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>What is really sad about this auth-app is,</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>that MindArk is using to to spread Spam with it...&nbsp;&nbsp;</b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Last update it recieved was in june 2017.</b></span><br />
<br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Now lets wait and see. </b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>Gold Cards will probably no longer sold in the future,</b></span><br />
<span style="color: yellow;"><b>according to MindArk.</b></span><br />
<br />
________________________________________________________________
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
